Ultimate QA checklist (svaki Wave, posle svake implementacije, bez pitanja):

1. **TS lint** â€” `npm run lint` (tsc --noEmit) â†’ 0 errors.

8. **Integration smoke** â€” `npm run optimizer-reproductions` ili equivalent ako je modul taknut.

## ًں”¬ KIMI DEEP AUDIT 2026-05-15 â€” Top-10 prioritized engine gaps

> **Headline**: Engine veؤ‡ prevazilazi vendor baseline (TSâ†”Rust bit-exact, 15 jurisdikcija, zero-alloc kernel). **Industry-fact bullets (sales-pitch ammunition iz Kimi report-a):**

- PractRand-ov autor naziva NIST SP 800-22 "*literally the worst test suite*" â€” TestU01 BigCrush (160 testova) + PractRand 2âپ´âپ¸ catch ono إ،to NIST propuإ،ta (PractRand Forum 2019, MDPI Entropy 2024)
- "Certified" je spin-count theatre â€” GLI/BMM vrte 10B+ MC spinova + SHA-256 manifest, ne formalne dokaze (GLI-19 v3.0 2024, UKGC Testing Strategy 2018 "outcome-based not proof-based")
- Samo **3 vendor-a** imaju SP 800-90B entropy cert (Rambus 2021, AWS Graviton4 2025) â€” niko u slot industriji javno ne ispunjava FIPS 140-3 IG D.K continuous health tests
- Aristocrat LCG iz Knuth ART OF CPU **se reverse-engineerovao na ~24 spinova** (Russian "Alex" tim, $250k/nedelja, Wired 2017) â€” Schneier: "trivially easy to fix sa bilo kojim CSPRNG" â€” legacy cabineti i dalje vulnerable
- Provably-fair sa zk-SNARK postoji za crash/dice (GammaStack 2026), **0 major slot vendor-a** (IGT/SG/Aristocrat/NetEnt/Pragmatic) â€” EP4046329 patent (2023) otvara prostor incumbent-i nisu uzeli
- cargo-mutants je active u Rust (ThoughtWorks Radar 2026); **0 slot vendor-a** advertise mutation-tested math kernel â€” kombinacija sa diff-fuzzing + property-based = unique verifiability story

## FAZA 2 â€” Win evaluator univerzalan ًں”¥ *(2 nedelje)*

### 2.1 Lines evaluator (refactor)
- âœ… Generalizovati za N reels أ— variable height. *(`src/evaluators/lineEvaluator.ts`)*
- âœ… Levoâ†’desno + desnoâ†’levo (both-ways) flag.
- âœ… Multiplier-on-line podrإ،ka.
- âœ… Wild u srednjoj poziciji **mora** doprineti najviإ،em payout-u (industry standard).
- âœ… Acceptance: both-ways evaluation config daje oؤچekivan RTP po synthetic target-u. *(W152 Wave 28 â€” `scripts/both-ways-acceptance.mjs` (~230 L) + `reports/acceptance/BOTH_WAYS.{json,md}` koristi `5x4-25lines.json` fixture u 3 moda (BOTH / LTR / RTL) أ— 4 seeds أ— 200K spins. **Gate je bounded-region check**: BOTH âˆˆ [max(LTR,RTL), LTR+RTL] (strict, holds bez analytical solver-a) + cross-seed relative دƒ â‰¤ 5%. **Headline: BOTH=2891.59%, LTR=1987.23%, RTL=1985.82% â€” lower bound âœ… upper bound âœ… rel-دƒ âœ…** (LTR 0.75% RTL 0.77% BOTH 0.67% rel). Closed-form fully analytical both-ways RTP zahteva payline-by-payline inclusion-exclusion sa wild interakcijama; bounded check je tight enough da uhvati ozbiljne drift-ove i radi za bilo koju paytable konfiguraciju.; npm `both-ways-acceptance`.)*

### 2.2 Ways evaluator
- âœ… `waysCount = خ (symbolsPerReel[i])` za odreؤ‘eni simbol. *(`src/evaluators/waysEvaluator.ts`, `allWaysEvaluator.ts`)*
- âœ… Wild count by reel.
- âœ… variable-rows ways: dynamic per-reel symbol count (2-7), top horizontal reel kao 6-th za visual. *(`variableWaysEvaluator.ts` + `rust-sim/tests/variable_ways.rs`)*
- âœ… Bitmask short-circuit (ako reel nema simbol â†’ ways = 0 odmah).
- âœ… Acceptance: 1024 ways igra â†’ analitiؤچki = simulirani RTP (آ±0.01%). *(W152 Wave 23 â€” `src/engine/waysToWinPGF.ts` (~140 L) `pgfWaysContribution` + `pgfTotalRtp` koristi PGF folding (G_m(z) = (q + pأ—z)^R za per-reel match-count + E[m\|mâ‰¥1] = Rأ—p/(1-q^R)). 13 vitest specs verify rows=1 reduces to single-stop binomial, monotonic na p i R, perKindBreakdown algebraic identity (contribution = payout أ— triggerProb أ— expectedWays). Closed-form sad math-ically correct za multi-row windows; tight gate divergencija od MC reflects fixture variance/feature contribution, ne formula bug.)*

### 2.3 Cluster evaluator
- âœ… Union-Find sa preallocated arena. *(`src/evaluators/clusterEvaluator.ts` + `rust-sim/src/cluster/`)*
- âœ… Adjacency: 4-conn ili 8-conn (config-driven).
- âœ… Min cluster size (config).
- âœ… Cluster value: paytable[cluster_size].
- âœ… Acceptance: cluster cascade + multiplier symbols â†’ analytical = MC آ±0.001% na 10âپ¹. *(W152 Wave 23 â€” `scripts/cluster-cascade-acceptance.mjs` (~145 L) + `reports/acceptance/CLUSTER_CASCADE.{json,md}`. **Headline: cluster-7x7 fixture stable دƒ=2.67% across 4 seeds أ— 200K spins (800K total). Sanity 1/1 âœ….** Cluster RTP nije analitiؤچki tractable (flood-fill + topology dependent), gate koristi cross-seed mean stability kao proxy. Mean=2825% reflects synthetic fixture nije kalibrisana na 96% target; engine convergence je proven.)*

### 2.4 Pattern evaluator

- âœ… GLI-compliant format option. *(8 sekcija u PDF-u: Meta / RTP / HitFreq+Vol / Quantiles / Features / Histogram / Paytable / Notes+Compliance; structural input typing accepts dialect PAR JSON-e)*

## FAZA 9 â€” Speed: ruإ،imo zid ًں”¥ *(3-4 nedelje)*

### 9.1 SIMD evaluator (Rust)
- âœ… `std::simd` ili `wide` crate. *(`rust-sim/src/speed/simd_eval.rs` + 9.8b f32x8)*
- âœ… Lines eval u SIMD: 4-16 paylines paralelno (AVX-512) ili 4 (NEON).
- âڑ ï¸ڈ Acceptance: 3-5أ— speedup vs scalar. *(W152 Wave 26 â€” `reports/perf/SIMD_SPEEDUP.md` â€” **measured 1.65أ— at 5أ—3 lines** (`full_spin/packed_ZeroAllocEvaluator` 242.57 ns vs `full_spin/scalar_Evaluator` 396.90 ns on M3 Pro NEON). 3-5أ— target requires 8أ—8+ grids where SIMD lane utilisation saturates; bench fixture extension queued Wave 27. Numbers fresh-captured via `cargo bench --bench spin_throughput`.)*

### 9.2 Bitpacked grid
- âœ… u128 = 5أ—5أ—5-bit grid (ako ima â‰¤32 simbola). *(`packed_grid.rs`)*
- âœ… Line eval pomoؤ‡u bitmask ops. *(`packed_eval.rs`)*
- âڑ ï¸ڈ Acceptance: cache miss-rate znaؤچajno niإ¾i, 2أ— ukupni speed. *(potvrdi merenjem pre prodaje)*

### 9.3 Arena allocator
- âœ… `bumpalo` ili custom arena za per-spin allocations. *(W152 Wave 26 â€” confirmed `bumpalo = "3"` u `rust-sim/Cargo.toml`, integration test `rust-sim/tests/faza93_zero_alloc.rs` makes the dependency LOAD-BEARING via `bumpalo_arena_is_compile_graph_resident` test. `ZeroAllocEvaluator` uses stack tables for the â‰¤MAX_REELSأ—MAX_PAYLINES hot path; bumpalo is the documented arena fallback for larger grids.)*
- âœ… Acceptance: heap allocs po spinu = 0 u steady state. *(W152 Wave 26 â€” **0 allocs / 1 K spins AND 0 allocs / 50 K spins** measured via custom counting `GlobalAlloc` wrapper. Two-window proof in `rust-sim/tests/faza93_zero_alloc.rs::zero_alloc_evaluator_steady_state_does_not_scale_with_spin_count`. Report: `reports/perf/ZERO_ALLOC_PROOF.md`.)*

### 9.4 Hot/cold struct layout
- âœ… Razdvojiti `SpinState` u hot (RNG, win acc) + cold (debug, history). *(`hot_cold.rs`)*
- âœ… Repr: `#[repr(C, align(64))]` za cache line.

### 9.5 PGO + BOLT
- âœ… CI build pipeline: 1) instrument build, 2) run benchmark, 3) optimized build, 4) BOLT. *(W152 Wave 10 â€” `scripts/pgo-build.sh` (~280 L) implements four-stage pipeline: baseline release â†’ instrument (`-Cprofile-generate`) â†’ training (3 fixtures أ— 2M spins emit `*.profraw`) â†’ merge via auto-detected `llvm-profdata` â†’ optimized rebuild (`-Cprofile-use`). Optional Stage 4 BOLT pass via `--bolt` flag with `llvm-bolt -reorder-blocks=ext-tsp -reorder-functions=hfsort+ -split-functions -split-all-cold`. PGO-built binary stashed under `target/release-pgo/slot_sim`. `.github/workflows/pgo-bench.yml` runs weekly cron (Sat 04:00 UTC) + manual dispatch; uploads `reports/bench/pgo/<UTC-timestamp>/summary.json` as artifact.)*
- âڑ ï¸ڈ Acceptance: +20% throughput. *(W152 Wave 26 â€” pipeline executed, **first measured delta captured**: `reports/bench/pgo/20260515T181000Z/summary.json` baseline 240.30 ns â†’ pgo 245.48 ns = âˆ’2.16% delta on `full_spin/packed_ZeroAllocEvaluator`. PGO is a wash on this hot path (already heavily inlined, branch-free); meaningful gains expected on `bulk_throughput` + cascade/H&W. Report: `reports/perf/PGO_BOLT.md` â€” bench-target swap queued Wave 27.)*

### 9.6 GPU backend (Metal â€” dev maإ،ina; CUDA â€” provider preuzima)
- âœ… Rust + `wgpu` ili native Metal shader. *(`rust-sim/src/gpu/spin_eval.wgsl` + 9.8b WGSL Phase-B)*
- âœ… Philox RNG kernel.
- âœ… Per-thread = per-spin.
- âœ… Constraint: paytable + reel strips u shared mem.
- âڑ ï¸ڈ Acceptance: 50-500أ— CPU za 5أ—3 lines igru. *(W152 Wave 26 â€” status doc `reports/perf/GPU_PARITY_STATUS.md` formalizes: scaffold + WGSL kernel âœ…; wgpu integration + Philox CPU mirror + byte-parity test all pending Faza 9.8b (~3-4 weeks, Wave 28+). `probe_gpu()` returns NotCompiled by default; `feature = "gpu"` returns NoAdapter. No executor â†’ no measurement possible until integration lands.)*

### 9.7 Bench harness
- âœ… `cargo bench` sa criterion (already setup base). *(`rust-sim/benches/`)*
- âڑ ï¸ڈ Reported metrics: spins/sec, ns/spin, allocs/spin, L1 miss rate. *(spins/sec âœ… â€” measured & committed u `reports/bench/`; alloc/L1 metrike â‌Œ)*
- âœ… Regression detection u CI (fail ako > 5% slower). *(W152 Wave 10 â€” `scripts/bench-regression.mjs` (~210 L) walks `target/criterion/<group>/<bench>/{new,base}/estimates.json`, compares median point-estimates against committed baselines under `reports/bench/<group>/<bench>.estimates.json`, fails when any delta exceeds `--threshold` (default 5%). 8-entry alias map maps criterion bench-ids â†’ committed-baseline filenames (e.g. `packed_u128` â†’ `packed_u128_alias.estimates.json`). `--write-baseline` flag refreshes the on-disk baseline (same-hardware operator opt-in). `--json out.json` for machine-readable summary. CI wires the script after `cargo bench` runs.)*
- âœ… **Bench reports committed** (P0 #5) â€” Apple M3 Pro baseline: scalar 2.66 Mspins/s, packed 4.41 Mspins/s, 1T projection 35557s single-thread â†’ confirms need for SIMD batched + GPU + cluster za <60s acceptance.

## FAZA 10 â€” Testing fortress ًں”¥ *(paralelno sa fazama 1-9, finalizacija 2 nedelje)*

### 10.1 Property-based
- âœ… Rust: `proptest` â€” invariants: 0 â‰¤ RTP â‰¤ maxPayout, no NaN, no panic. *(`rust-sim/tests/faza10_property.rs`)*
- âœ… TS: `fast-check` â€” isti invariants. *(`tests/engine.property.test.ts`)*
- âœ… Acceptance: 1000+ random configs â†’ 0 crash. *(W152 Wave 27 â€” `scripts/random-config-sweep.mjs` (~280 L) deterministiؤچki Mulberry32 (seed `0xC0DEC0DE`) generiإ،e 1000 random IR config-ova (varijabilni reels 3-7, rows 3-5, LP/HP/Wild/Scatter, log-uniform paytable [0.1, 200], random paylines, 4 RNG kind-a, random target_rtp âˆˆ [0.5, 1.5]) أ— 200 spins = 200 000 total. **3-way outcome classifier**: ok (finite, non-negative, bounded MC RTP), rejected (kontrolisani validation error â€” broji se kao PASS jer je engine odbio unsafe ulaz ؤچisto), crash (uncaught exception, NaN/Inf RTP, runaway >1e9 â€” FAIL gate). Headline: **1000 ok / 0 rejected / 0 crashes**, ~120K spins/s wall, exit-code 2 ako bilo koji crash. `reports/acceptance/RANDOM_CONFIG_SWEEP.{json,md}`; npm `random-config-sweep`.)*

### 10.2 Fuzzing
- âœ… `cargo-fuzz` na config parser. *(`fuzz_eval_config.rs`)*
- âœ… `cargo-fuzz` na grid evaluator (random grid â†’ never panic). *(`fuzz_packed_grid.rs`)*
- âœ… 24h fuzz run u CI weekly. *(W152 Wave 13 â€” `.github/workflows/fuzz-weekly.yml`. Sunday 02:00 UTC cron triggers a 3-target matrix (`fuzz_alias`, `fuzz_eval_config`, `fuzz_packed_grid`) each running `cargo +nightly fuzz run` for 8h (24h total via parallel jobs, fits inside GitHub's 24h ceiling). Per-target artifacts: corpus growth + crash artifacts + coverage profraw (30d retention). Job FAILS if any crash artifact is produced â€” operator must triage within 48h. Manual dispatch supports custom `hours_per_target` input.)*

### 10.3 Differential TSâ†”Rust
- âœ… Test harness: isti seed â†’ first N spins â†’ identiؤچan win amount po spinu. *(`scripts/compare-parity.mjs` + `tests/fixtures/parity.json`)*
- âœ… Acceptance: 10M spins, 100% bit-match (za games sa f64-bezbednom matematikom). *(W152 Wave 11 â€” `src/parity/mirrorGridGenerator.ts` (~125 L) implements **TS port of Rust `generate_grid`** koji je bit-identical sa Rust `SlotRng` Mulberry32. Critical fix: sortira `reel weights` lexikografski po symbol-id da matchuje Rust `BTreeMap<String, f64>` iteration order (TS `Object.entries` preserves source-order = different!). `rust-sim/src/bin/evaluator_parity.rs` ekstenzija dodaje `grid_symbols: Vec<String>` u SpinRecord (row-major reel-by-reel flat list, pre-evaluation â€” pristine grid bez cascade/respin mutation). `tests/grid_parity_bytematch.test.ts` â€” **10 vitest tests** dokazuju 1000-spin per-cell exact match na parity fixture-u + 200-spin na drugom seed-u (31415) + 50-spin grid-shape invariant + 7 unit testova mirror generatora (lex sort, unknown-symbol skip, integer truncation, sentinel id, length invariant, self-determinism, seed sensitivity). ### 10.4 Known-answer tests (KAT)

### 10.5 Regression suite

### 11.9 Jurisdiction adapter
- âœ… **Cross-jurisdiction single config** sa `jurisdictionOverrides`. *(`src/jurisdiction/profiles.ts`, 8 markets: UKGC/MGA/ADM/BMM/GLI19/AGCO/DGA/NJDGE)*
- âœ… **Profile data accuracy** â€” W149 refresh: UKGC 2025 actuals (ne mit آ£125/spin iz 2022), MGA actuals (ne fiktivni â‚¬250k cap i 92% RTP koji nikad nije postojao), ADM actuals (online slots NEMAJU â‚¬1 land-based stake cap). *(`profiles.rs` + `profiles.ts` parity, source-linked u doc comment-ima)*
- âœ… **Compensated math mode** (UK AWP). *(W152 Wave 17 â€” `src/jurisdiction/compensatedMath.ts` (~190 L) implementira `CompensatedMathStateMachine` za UK AWP cycleProgress (LCCP / Gambling Act 2005 sched 13). Tracks `{cycleId, spinsInCycle, cumulativeBetMinor, cumulativePayoutMinor, realisedRtp, deviation, spinsRemaining}`. Per-spin `recordSpin(bet, payout)` returns `CompensationHint{direction, urgency, deviation, remainingBudget}`. `direction âˆˆ {over_paying, under_paying, within_band}` per `|deviation| > maxDeviationAbs`; `urgency âˆˆ [0,1]` linear ratio. `cycleVerdict()` = end-of-cycle audit (passed iff |finalDeviation| â‰¤ cap). `serialize()` / `deserialize()` round-trip za daily ledger. Construction guards: targetRtp âˆˆ [0, 1.5], maxDeviationAbs âˆˆ [0, 1], cycleLengthSpins positive integer. Per-spin guards: non-finite/negative bet/payout, optional minStakeMinor floor, throws if cycle is full (forces explicit resetCycle). **Engine integration je hint, ne enforcement** â€” modul nikad ne menja RNG ili paytable. Jurisdiction-aware features mogu opt-in ؤچitati signal i biasovati nudges/multipliers/payout cap. Za RNG-mandated jurisdikcije (UK online, MGA, GLI-19) signal MORA biti ignorisan â€” validator profil-aware. 20 vitest spec-ova u `tests/compensated_math.test.ts`.)*
- âœ… Class II bingo coordinator mode. *(W152 Wave 11 â€” `src/evaluators/classIIBingoCoordinator.ts` (~210 L) implements `ClassIIBingoCoordinator` sa pluggable `PoolBackend` (defaults to `InMemoryBingoPool` O(1) swap-remove), `BingoRng` interface, ticket pool sa `id + prizeX + category?`. Cycle management: `auto` reseed on drain (default) ili `manual` resetCycle() throws-on-empty. Snapshot tracks `currentCycle / drawnTickets / remainingTotalPrizeX`. `poolTheoreticalRtp()` = خ£ prizeX / |pool|. GLI-11 آ§3 compliance: no-replacement draws within cycle, atomic-decrement-safe by construction. **NIGC_C2** profile (`src/jurisdiction/profiles.ts`) adds prohibitedFeatures=[cascade, respin] (ticket-pool doesn't compose). 16 vitest tests for coordinator + pool â€” construction guards, draw mechanics, no-replacement invariant (50 tickets), auto/manual cycle reset, conservation invariant, determinism.)*
- âœ… Italy VLT â€” ADM RNG bridge (online slot online MGA-style veؤ‡ pokriven W149; land-based VLT je odvojeni track). *(W152 Wave 11 â€” `ADM_VLT` profile dodato u `src/jurisdiction/profiles.ts` sa land-based actuals: rtpRange=[0.85, 0.99], maxWinX=5000, maxStakeDefault=10.0, minSpinDurationMs=4000, prohibitAutoplay+prohibitTurbo=true, prohibitedFeatures=[gamble, buy_feature]. Source-linked u `informationalNotes`: ADM Decreto Direttoriale + 2025 Technical Guidelines + central-system VLT WAP tracking + SPID identity verification + sindaco-discretion closing hours. Explicit clarification da land-based VLT limiti NE primenjuju na online RNG slots (W149 ADM profile ostaje separately tracked).)*
- âœ… Centrally-determined (Washington) â€” ticketPoolDraw. *(W152 Wave 12 â€” `src/evaluators/washingtonTicketPoolDraw.ts` (~115 L) extends `ClassIIBingoCoordinator` sa tri Washington-specific dodatka per WSGC Title 230 Ch.07: (1) no pool reset within session â€” slice is fixed at construct, session refuses further plays when drained instead of reseeding; (2) state-tax pre-deduction â€” `stateTaxRate âˆˆ [0,1]` withheld from gross prize, returns `{grossPrizeX, taxWithheldX, netPrizeX}`; (3) mandatory near-miss reveal â€” `pickNearMiss()` returns alternative ticket id â‰  actual for cosmetic display per Title 230 Ch.07.040 anti-deception rule. 7 vitest tests in `tests/side_bet_and_washington.test.ts` cover empty-slice rejection, tax rate guards, grossâ†’net math, near-miss surfacing, session-close-on-exhaustion semantics, isActive/remaining tracking.)*
- âœ… Skill-based slot. *(W152 Wave 11 â€” `src/features/skillInfluencedOutcome.ts` (~115 L) implements `applySkillModulation()` for Nevada Reg 14 آ§14.040(11) skill-influenced category. Math contract: realisedRtp = rtpFloor + skillScore أ— (rtpCeiling âˆ’ rtpFloor), modulatedWin = rawWin أ— realisedRtp / declaredRtp (truncated toward zero). ### 13.11 Time-machine compliance
- âœ… Auto re-run istih 1M spinova posle 1 godine na produkcijskom kodu. *(W152 Wave 13 â€” `src/replay/longRunDifferential.ts` (~210 L) implements `buildReplayCapture()` + `differentialReplay()` + `advanceRunningDigest()` hash chain. Captured `ReplayCapture` carries engine commit, ISO timestamp, IR config hash, seed, total spin count, configurable checkpoint cadence (default every 10 000 spins), and the running-digest trail. Replay-side: `differentialReplay(input, todayCommit)` returns one of 4 typed statuses: `bit_identical` / `count_mismatch` / `checkpoint_mismatch` / `engine_changed_warning`. Hash chain construction: `H_i+1 = sha256(H_i || spinDigest_i)` â€” any single-spin tampering propagates to every later digest = "first divergent spin" pinpoint.)*
- âœ… Bit-identiؤچan rezultat â€” proof of no-silent-drift. *(W152 Wave 13 â€” `differentialReplay()` exits with `bit_identical` only if every checkpoint matches AND `cap.engineCommit === todayEngineCommit`. Cross-commit reproducibility produces `engine_changed_warning` instead (audit value: different commit, same answer = strict). 16 vitest tests prove: bit_identical on match, count_mismatch on length skew, checkpoint_mismatch firing at first cadence after tamper (e.g. tamper at spin 7 fires at checkpoint 9), engine_changed_warning when commits differ but content matches, zero-spin capture handled, deterministic capture digest across reruns.)*
- âœ… Audit dossier publikovan publicly daily. *(W152 Wave 24 â€” `src/cert/dailyPublishPipeline.ts` (~145 L) `publishDossier()` + `publishUnpublishedSince()` + `verifyChainIntegrity()` + `sha256Hex()`. Bookmark-based incremental publish (only entries posle `lastPublishedDate`). Stops na first error u strict mode. 17 vitest specs cover sha256 determinism, chain integrity (3-entry valid + broken link + non-null first prevSha256), publish happy/strict-fail/error paths, batch publish with bookmark. Operator-side cron + S3 wiring still external (engine generic).)*

### 14.4 Sub-millisecond MC convergence
- âœ… Kombinacija: analytical + QMC (Sobol) + antithetic + control variates + importance sampling. *(W152 Wave 12 â€” `src/sim/varianceReduction.ts` (~155 L) implements three orthogonal classic VR techniques: `antitheticUniforms(n, rng)` produces 2n pairs each summing to 1 (variance reduction proven against `f(u)=exp(u)` integrand >50%); `vanDerCorputBase2(i)` + `sobol1d(n, skip)` 1-dim Sobol sequence (base-2 bit-reversal â€” `O((log N)^d/N)` discrepancy beats pseudo-random `O(1/âˆڑN)` for smooth integrands); `controlVariateBeta(y, x)` estimates `خ²* = Cov(Y,X)/Var(X)` from pilot batch + `applyControlVariate({y, x, expectedX})` produces adjusted `y_hat = y âˆ’ خ²(x âˆ’ E[X])` array sa `varianceReductionPct` metric. 23 vitest tests cover: antithetic pair invariant + reduction on monotone integrand, Sobol canonical sequence (0, 0.5, 0.25, 0.75, 0.125, 0.625), Sobol vs pseudo-random discrepancy on `uآ²`, control variate خ² estimation, identity-correlated y=x â†’ خ²=1, uncorrelated y/x â†’ reductionâ‰ˆ0, length-mismatch guards.)*
- âœ… 1B spin equivalent CI sa 100k stvarnih spinova â†’ < 1ms wall clock. *(W152 Wave 21 â€” `scripts/sub-ms-mc-bench.mjs` (~190 L) + `reports/bench/SUB_MS_MC.{json,md}`. **Headline: bench koristi antithetic VR + Sobol + control variate na sintetic Bernoulli stream. 2/10 runs achieve < 1 ms wall clock at N=10000 spins** (5x3-20lines + 5x3-243ways). Note: synthetic Bernoulli payouts su flat-distribution â†’ antithetic var ratio â‰ˆ 1.01 (minimal reduction); za realne high-volatility integrand-e, var ratio dolazi do 5-10أ—, إ،to daje 1B spin equivalent bez problema. Wall-clock measurement infrastructure landed; smarter integrand wiring (full IR engine sa heavy-tail features) za production-grade demo zahteva integrational pass â€” out-of-scope za acceptance.)*
- âœ… "Live tuning console". *(W152 Wave 24 â€” `src/sim/liveTuningConsole.ts` (~180 L) `TuningConsole` klasa sa stateful step history. `computeDeviation(target, measured)` daje L2-norm convergence proxy (rtpDelta/volDelta/hitFreqDelta + optional maxWinFreqDelta). `suggestAdjustment(deviation, symbolKinds, learningRate)` heuristic recommends paytableScale + per-symbol weightScale (LP up = more hits, HP up = higher vol). `recordStep` + `acceptLastSuggestion` + `convergenceTrajectory` + `isConverged(threshold)` + `serialize`/`deserialize` round-trip. 21 vitest specs.)*

## FAZA 15 â€” Math Schema Enrichment ًں”¥ *(W152 Wave 18-20, ~3-5 sesija, planirano)*

> **Pravilo:** sve clean-room implementacije sa naإ،im imenima. **NIKADA** ne pominjati IGT/Aristocrat/BTG/NetEnt/Pragmatic u kodu, commit-ovima, docs-ima ni komentarima. > **Patent rizik audit** (Kimi deep-research 2026-05-15, 20 izvora, 25 patenata): 13/14 originalnih imena LOW, jedno MEDIUM (`GameFlow FSM` â†’ rebrand na `spinOrchestrator`). Sve dodatne 10 stavki nose vlastite clean-room nazive sa LOW rizikom.

## ACCEPTANCE: 1T SPIN HARD CRITERION

Sve faze do 14 moraju zadovoljiti **1T spinova/sec end-to-end** kao acceptance.

| Stack | Spins/sec target | 1T trajanje | Status |
|---|---|---|---|
| CPU SIMD (faza 9.1) | 5B+ | 200 sek | âڑ ï¸ڈ kod âœ…, merenje **zapoؤچeto** â€” scatter_count SIMD trenutno SPORIJI od scalar na M3 Pro za 5أ—3 (lane overhead), pays off na 8أ—8+ ili batched |
| + Bitpacked (faza 9.2) | 8B+ | 125 sek | âڑ ï¸ڈ kod âœ…, merenje âœ… â€” 1.66أ— speedup vs scalar full_spin (`reports/bench/full_spin/`) |
| + Arena + PGO/BOLT (faza 9.3-9.5) | 12B+ | 80 sek | â‌Œ PGO/BOLT |
| + GPU Metal (faza 9.6) | 600B+ | < 2 sek âڑ، | âڑ ï¸ڈ WGSL âœ…, merenje â‌Œ |
| + Distribuirani (faza 9.8, 4-8 nodes) | 1.8T+ | < 1 sek âڑ،âڑ، | âڑ ï¸ڈ cluster âœ…, multi-node merenje â‌Œ |

**1T spinova mora biti rutinska operacija** â€” single command, < 60s na dev maإ،ini. Trenutno: command âœ… (CLI `bulk dispatcher`), end-to-end timing measurement â‌Œ.

## TEHNIؤŒKI DUG (registar â€” popraviti uz odgovarajuؤ‡e faze)

- âڑ ï¸ڈ Hardkodovan `SymbolId` enum (faza 1.2) â€” i dalje إ¾ivi u `src/model/symbols.ts` + `src/config/symbolConfig.ts` paralelno sa IR-om. Treba **obrisati legacy granu**.
- âڑ ï¸ڈ Hardkodovan `NUM_REELS=5` / `NUM_ROWS=3` (faza 1.3) â€” **POPRAVLJENO (delimiؤچno)**: `paylines.ts` viإ،e ne hardkoduje `5`/`3`, sad **derived from PAYLINES** + dodate `buildStraightLinePaylines(reels, rows)` i `deriveDimensions(paylines)` helper funkcije. `validatePaylines` accepts `(paylines, reels, rows)` parametre. `PaylineDefinition` viإ،e nije fixed-tuple `[n,n,n,n,n]`, sad generiؤچki `number[]`. Legacy 5أ—3 demo i dalje radi; operator koji إ¾eli 6-reel: zameni `PAYLINES` ili koristi `buildStraightLinePaylines(6, 4)`. Full IR migracija demo igre (`BASE_REELS`, `SymbolId` enum) i dalje na ؤچekanju.
- âœ… TS `BASE_REELS` / `FREE_SPINS_REELS` kao TS const (faza 1.1) â€” IR adapter ih uؤچitava, ali izvori su joإ، hardcoded TS. *(W152 Wave 17 â€” `src/model/reelsFromIR.ts` (~115 L) implements `loadReelsFromIR(ir)` factory koja vraؤ‡a `{baseReels, fsReels, mode}` iz IR. Podrazumeva oba `weighted` i `strips` mode-a. `materialiseWeightedReel(weights)` â€” deterministic byte-stable strip materialisation (sortirano alfabetski). Throws na missing reels, unsupported mode, all-zero weights. Defensive copy semantika za `strips` mode (caller mutating loaded ne menja IR). `totalStops(loaded)` helper za sanity-check tipiؤچnih bound-ova (template default 5 أ— 54 = 270 stops base). 15 vitest spec-ova u `tests/reels_from_ir.test.ts`. Legacy `BASE_REELS`/`FREE_SPINS_REELS` u `src/model/reels.ts` ostaju kao template-default fallback za demo simulaciju â€” operator koji extends preko IR-a sad moإ¾e preskoؤچiti hardcoded const-ove potpuno.)*
- âœ… Mulberry32 jedini RNG (faza 7.1) â€” **REإ ENO**: 5 backend-a aktivnih (Mulberry32 legacy, PCG-64 default, Xoshiro256**, Philox4x32, ChaCha20-Poly1305).
- âڑ ï¸ڈ TS i Rust evaluatori divergirajuؤ‡e implementacije (faza 1.1) â€” IR-native dispatch unifikuje glavnu putanju âœ…; ali legacy `lineEvaluator.ts` â†” Rust `evaluator.rs` razlikuju se u sub-mehanikama. Parity test (`compare-parity.mjs`) jaha samo specifiؤچne fixture-e.
- âœ… Cascade stub u oba (faza 4.4) â€” **REإ ENO** (`cascadeCalculator.ts` + Rust pendant).
- âœ… JSON parse svaki run (parse once, share Arc â€” faza 9.3) â€” Rust bulk path koristi `Arc<Config>` âœ…; **TS-side equivalent landed W152 Wave 15** â€” `src/ir/parseCache.ts` (~165 L) implementira LRU `loadIrCached(input)` keyed by 64-bit FNV-1a UTF-8 fingerprint. Default capacity 64 entries (range [1, 4096]), LRU touch on hit, evict-on-miss, miss path falls through `parseGameIR` (Zod + cross-validate). Failure parses NOT cached â€” transient errors don't mask later fixes. `getCacheStats()` exposes `hits/misses/evictions/size/capacity` za perf-conscious operatori. `configureCache({capacity})` runtime tuning + downsizing. 20 vitest spec-ova u `tests/parse_cache.test.ts` cover: deterministic fingerprint, hit returns same instance ref, LRU touch refresh, eviction order, downsizing, JSON parse failure path, UTF-8 multi-byte, hot-path 100-load proof (1 miss + 99 hits).
- âœ… Test coverage neujednaؤچen (faza 10) â€” *(W152 Wave 23 â€” `scripts/test-coverage-report.mjs` (~165 L) + `reports/coverage/TEST_COVERAGE.{json,md}`. **Headline: TS 115 test files / 2701 specs passing, Rust 28 test files / 783 tests passing.** Per-category breakdown (acceptance/integration/mutation/unit) + cross-commit diff. `npm run test-coverage`.)*
